| <span data-ttu-id="f8335-463">Voce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8335-463">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f8335-464">Valore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8335-464">Value</span></span> |
|-----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|

<span data-ttu-id="f8335-1665">La classe **MS-DFSR-Connection** fa parte del supporto del servizio di replica file System distribuito (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8335-1665">The **ms-DFSR-Connection** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
